    function readCookie(cname) {
        var name = cname + "=";
        try {
            var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
        } catch(err) {
            var decodedCookie = unescape(document.cookie);
        }
        var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
        for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1);
         }
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
            return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
            }
        return "";
        }

        function getparamVal(cookieStr, key) {
        if (cookieStr > "") {
        var val = "|" + cookieStr + "|";
        var pattern = new RegExp(".*?\\|" + key + "=([^|]*).*|.*");
        return val.replace(pattern, '$1');
        } else {
        return "";
            }
        }

function hdr_getusercity(city){
    var city =city||"All India";
    city=(city==''||city=="null"||city==null)?'All India':city;
    city=city.replace('-', ' ');
    var splitcity = city.toLowerCase().split(' ');
    for (var i = 0; i < splitcity.length; i++) {
        splitcity[i] = splitcity[i].charAt(0).toUpperCase() + splitcity[i].substring(1);  
    }

function setHdCountry()
{
    var hdIploc='',hdCcode='';
    var hdSrch="iploc=";
    if (document.cookie.length > 0){
        var offset = document.cookie.indexOf(hdSrch);
        if (offset != -1){
            offset += hdSrch.length;
            end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", offset);
            if (end == -1)
                end = document.cookie.length;
            hdIploc=unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, end));
        }
    }
    if(hdIploc != '' && hdIploc.indexOf('gcniso=') != -1){
   
        var hdcon = hdIploc.split('gcniso=');
        if(typeof(hdcon[1])!="undefined")
            var hdcarr = hdcon[1].split('|');
        hdCcode= hdcarr[0];
    }
    if(hdCcode == '')
    {
        var hdDate = new Date();
        var hdgmt = -hdDate.getTimezoneOffset() / 60;
        if (hdgmt != 5.5)
            hdCcode = 'OTHER';
        else
            hdCcode = 'IN';
    }
    if(typeof(hdCcode)!="undefined" && hdCcode != '' && hdCcode == 'IN')
    {
        var hdInpt = document.getElementsByClassName('duet');
        for (var i = 0, len = hdInpt.length; i < len; i++) {
            var hdMid = hdInpt[i];
            var hdContent = hdMid.innerHTML;
            if(hdContent.match(/^\+91/)){
                hdContent = hdContent.replace('+91-','0');
                hdMid.innerHTML=hdContent;
            }
        }
    }
    else if(typeof(hdCcode)!="undefined" && hdCcode != '' && hdCcode != 'IN')
    {
        var hdInpt = document.getElementsByClassName('duet');
        for (var i = 0, len = hdInpt.length; i < len; i++) {
            var hdMid = hdInpt[i];
            var hdContent = hdMid.innerHTML;
            if(hdContent.match(/^0/)){
                hdContent = hdContent.replace('0','+91-');
                hdMid.innerHTML=hdContent;
            }
        }
    }
}

                    function readCookie(cname) {
                    var name = cname + "=";
                    try {
                        var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
                    } catch(err) {
                        var decodedCookie = unescape(document.cookie);
                    }
                    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                    for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                        }
                        }
                    return "";
                    }

                    function getparamVal(cookieStr, key) {
                    if (cookieStr > "") {
                    var val = "|" + cookieStr + "|";
                    var pattern = new RegExp(".*?\\\|" + key + "=([^|]*).*|.*");
                    return val.replace(pattern, '\$1');
                    } else {
                    return "";
                        }
                    }

    /**

    function deleteCookieW3C(cname) {
        var d = new Date(); //Create an date object
        d.setTime(d.getTime() - (1000*60*60*24)); //Set the time to the past. 1000 milliseonds = 1 second
        var expires = "expires=" + d.toGMTString(); //Compose the expirartion date
        window.document.cookie = cname+"="+"; path=/; domain=.indiamart.com; "+expires ;//Set the cookie with name and the expiration date

    }
    //R cookiw will help to decide GCP host name
    //Now we are using GCP and DIR server
    function getCookieW3C(t){for(var n=t+"=",r=document.cookie.split(";"),e=0;e<r.length;e++){for(var i=r[e];" "==i.charAt(0);)i=i.substring(1);if(0==i.indexOf(n))return i.substring(n.length,i.length)}return""}
    var r_cookie = getCookieW3C('r');
    if(r_cookie != '' && r_cookie=='g'){

        r_cookie = 'unknown';

        return cleanedObj;

    function replaceNullWithEmptyStr(obj) {
        if (obj && typeof obj === 'object') {
            // Iterate over key-value pairs and replace null values with empty strings
            Object.entries(obj).forEach(([key, value]) => {
                obj[key] = value == null ? '' : value;
            });
        }
        return obj;
    }

    function getObject(row, relProdType) {
        const dd = new Date();
        const cr_dt = `${dd.getFullYear()}${(dd.getMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0')}${dd.getDate().toString().padStart(2, '0')}${dd.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0')}${dd.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0')}${dd.getSeconds().toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;

        let currObj = {
            id: row.DISPLAY_ID,
            propName: 'DIR',
            relProdType: relProdType,
            DT: cr_dt,
            c_name: row.COMPANYNAME,
            c_number: row.CONTACT_NUMBER,
            c_url: row.COMPANY_URL,
            c_w: row.CUSTTYPE_WEIGHT,

            fl_name: row.GLCAT_MCAT_FLNAME,
            img_250: row.IMAGE_250X250,

            price_f: row.PRICE_F,

            tscode: row.ETO_OFR_COMPANY_TSCODE,
        };

        return cleanedObj;
    }

    function saveRelData(prodArr) {
        if(prodArr.length==0) {
            return;
        }
        // prodArr- 5 products array

        let relProdArr = [];
        prodArr.forEach(row => {
            let cleanedObj = getObject(row, 'fr');

        });

        if(relProdArr.length != 0) {
            typeof(sugg.recent)!='undefined' && typeof(sugg.recent)=='function' && sugg.recent({rel_prod: relProdArr});
        }
    }
